# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
A 6 sided dice is rolled and only one six appears after 24 rolls.  Using a one-tailed test investigate whether or not the dice is biased. ^pfD3f38j

Test to a significance level of 5%. ^S1aDknya

In Luigi's restaurant, 1 in 10 order pinot grigio. In a sample of 50, 11 choose the pinot grigio. Luigi wants to know if the drink has become more popular.
Test to a significance level of 1% ^W9N3eFGp
